As a nod to Jordan's on-court play, the Men's Air Jordan Retro 5 Basketball Shoes were designed to look like a fighter plane. In the famed model, MJ earned his fourth consecutive scoring title, sixth All-Star appearance and led the Bulls to the Eastern Conference Finals.

MEN'S AIR JORDAN 5 RETRO 'TOP 3'

	Full-grain leather upper on the Air Jordan Retro 5
	Encapsulated Air-Sole units for responsive cushioning
	PU midsole for soft, plush cushioning
	Flex grooves help promote natural movement
	Herringbone outsole for traction
	The Air Jordan Retro 5 is imported


In 1990, Michael Jordan’s game was on the rise and few could match the way he attacked opponents on the court. As a nod to Jordan's on-court play, the Men's Air Jordan Retro 5 Basketball Shoes were designed to look like a fighter plane. In the famed model, MJ earned his fourth consecutive scoring title, sixth All-Star appearance and led the Bulls to the Eastern Conference Finals.
